Incroyable! Now, unpopular opinion alert! ğŸ¤ I understand the emotions but enough with the unfair comparisons, already guys. lol. Both of them are amazing! And this is coming from someone who bawled and bawled when I first heard Emma's Maastricht performance - and a few times thereafter. Haha. Surreal and haungtingly beautiful, I thought I'd never recover from it - and, at the time, I only understood just about a quarter of the lyrics. Watching her with Helen though, I don't hear why people say Emma's better. I just think they're different. Helene's voice is rich, full, vibrant, confident and silkier while Emma's is young, plaintive, tentative and expressive with its smallness and the little staccatos. Then, I think her voice is not completely broken yet - and that's part of the appeal for such a vulnerable song. Also - very importantly - Emma got practically all the places that lend themselves to the most expression and variation (especially because of sparse and less rigid (and a tad slower) instrumentation) e.g. the beginning, the start of "ne partez pas," the modulation, etc. That's intentional because she's the guest and star of the song. So the arrangement respects that and Helene lets the girl shine as she deserves to.   That said, I thought that first beautiful harmony after the modulation may have been a little premature. I would have loved to hear the new key established fully, revel in it and then a harmony might have carried a little more nuanced dynamism (I know!) when the scatting began. It felt like being in a fancy restaurant and the hors d'oeuvre is so good, you legit would eat just that but then the waiters come and take it away to bring the main course before you've even had the chance to open your eyes from that first bite. Don't come for me; the whole thing is perfection. This is just a little 'what if'. Then again, maybe they tried that already in rehearsal and it just didn't work? It may have required a little more rearrangement in other places, anyway. E.g. After that, then should the scatting have commenced with solos or harmony?   All the same, as the whole world has noted, this is an excellent performance by two people who just get it and have touched us all with their gift. Deep, deep respect!  Everyone says Emma's a fighter. No she's not; she's a victor! Her voice alone is a knockout to that thing and I hope she keeps kicking it in the face even on the most difficult days.

Reading all these comments make my brain melt.  1. Why is this a duet? - Because it has always been the WHOLE concept of this show that Helene gets the opportunity to sing with artists that she WANTS to sing with. Without that this performance wouldn't even exist and there are more than enough videos of Emma alone to watch. So complaining is so stupid. By the way Helene is one of Emma's idols and Emma herself wanted to sing with Helene as well. Saying that Helene wants to profit of Emma's hype is stupid too considering that Helene is one of the most successful female singers in the whole world actually and absolutely doesn't need it as she is not interested in gaining exposure outside of the German speaking market. If you are from there and never have heard of her you pretty much have to have been living under a rock. I don't think that you need more than one hand to count the artists that had appearances on her show and didn't perform with Helene. The only one that comes to my mind at this point was Andrea Berg in the first show 2011.  2. Helene can't sing. - ... Helene can sing more than well enough. This was one of so many acts of the whole evening and Helene has max. 2 weeks to rehears the whole show, probably much less. This was her first time singing in French publicly. So it's highly probable that Helene focused more on trying to pronounce the words as good as possible than on delivering emotions. Noone wants to butcher a language purely out of respect. I would have done the same. Emma is singing this one single song for months now. So it's clear that that alone gives her a huge advantage. More so this isn't even a contest. Helene doesn't try to show people that she is better than her partners. That's not her. Not in a single performance with other artists in the history of the show did she try to be the centre of that performance. Either it's equally shared or she even fills more of a supporting role and even more so when she sang with children. There she always gave them the spotlight.  3. Why did Helene wear this outfit? - For the most part of her career and especially in the last 6 years acrobatics have become a big part of Helene's artistry and so she did them in this show as well, in this outfit. So it has to be suitable for that. If you think this is ordinary, I beg you please, that is just your problem. Could there be a better outfit for this situation? Of course, but with all the planning of the show, the running order of acts and everything involved there have to be compromises.

What they are saying is, that in their own personal opinion, no one can sing the song better. Thus, it is that personâ€™s song. Another way to put it is, that it is their signature song, the one they are best known for. For example, there are several artists out there that when their name is mentioned, most people will think of the exact same song associated with that artist. Regardless of whether others have done the song before or afterwards and possibly did a nice job on it themselves, the one artist did such an outstanding job on it, that the song is now â€œtheirsâ€.
